Based on the edition by N. A. Jayawickrama: Vimànavatthu and Petavatthu,
London : Pali Text Society 1977.



Input by the Dhammakaya Foundation, Thailand, 1989-1996
[GRETIL-Version vom 20.2.2015]

This work is licensed under a Creative Commons Attribution-ShareAlike 4.0 International License.

These files are provided by courtesy of the Pali Text Society for
scholarly purposes only.
In principle they represent a digital edition (without revision or
correction) of the printed editions of the complete set of Pali
canonical texts published by the PTS. While they have been subject to a
process of checking, it should not be assumed that there is no
divergence from the printed editions and it is strongly recommended that
they are checked against the printed editions before quoting.

%<                                     1>%
                Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammàsambuddhassa.
                                 1 URAGAVAGGA
                                I-  URAGAVAGGA
                           #<1 Khettåpamapetavatthu\<*<1>*>/>#
#<Vv_I,1[=1].1>#    Khettåpamà arahanto dàyakà kassakåpamà
     bãjåpamaü deyyadhammaü etto\<*<2>*>/ nibbattate phalaü.  #<|| 1 ||>#
#<Vv_I,1[=1].2>#    Etaü\<*<3>*>/ bãjaü kasã\<*<4>*>/ khettaü petànaü dàyakassa ca,
     taü petà paribhu¤janti dàtà pu¤¤ena vaóóhati.  #<|| 2 ||>#
#<Vv_I,1[=1].3>#    Idh' eva kusalaü katvà pete ca pañipåjiya\<*<5>*>/
     sagga¤ ca kamati\<*<6>*>/ ññhànaü\<*<7>*>/ kammaü katvàna
bhaddakan ti.  #<|| 3 ||>#
                        khettåpamapetavatthu pañhamaü\<*<8>*>/

\<--------------------------------------------------------------------------
     1 As in Vv., all the verses are serially numbered to the end
        in this edition though it is not done so in C, R, T.
        The title too is given at the head as in B, N.
     2 R ogho
     3 R ogha-
     4 B, N kasi; R, T kasã-
     5 R -påjayaü; (B1) -påjaya
     6 (K), (B2) gamati
     7 R, T, PvA(B, R) ñhànaü
     8 pañhamaü, dutiyaü etc. are added to the title at the end of
        the vatthu as in B, N, (P), T to indicate which number of
        the vagga each piece is. C, R have it indicated at the head.
>/

%<2                                   Petavatthu>%
                             #<2 Såkarapetavatthu>#
#<Vv_I,2[=2].1>#    Kàyo te sabbasovaõõo\<*<1>*>/ sabbà obhàsate disà
     mukhaü te såkarass' eva kiü kammam akarã\<*<2>*>/ pure ti.  #<|| 4 ||>#
#<Vv_I,2[=2].2>#    Kàyena sa¤¤ato àsiü vàcàyàsim\<*<3>*>/ asa¤¤ato
     tena me tàdiso vaõõo yathà passasi Nàrada.\<*<4>*>/  #<|| 5 ||>#
#<Vv_I,2[=2].3>#    Taü tyàhaü\<*<5>*>/ Nàrada bråmi sàmaü diññham idaü tayà
     màkàsi mukhasà pàpaü mà kho såkaramukho ahå ti.  #<|| 6 ||>#
                        Såkaramukhapetavatthu dutiyaü
\<&1>/
                            #<3 Påtimukhapetavatthu>#
#<Vv_I,3[=3].1>#        \<*<1>*>/Dibbaü subhaü dhàresi vaõõadhàtuü
         vehàyasaü\<*<2>*>/ tiññhasi antalikkhe\<*<3>*>/
         mukha¤ ca te kimayo\<*<4>*>/ påtigandhaü
         khàdanti, kiü kammam akàsi pubbe ti.  #<|| 7 ||>#
#<Vv_I,3[=3].2>#        \<*<1>*>/Samaõo ahaü pàpo 'tiduññhavàco\<*<5>*>/
         tapassiråpo\<*<6>*>/ mukhasà asa¤¤ato
         laddhà ca me tapasà vaõõadhàtu\<*<7>*>/
         mukha¤ ca me pesuõiyena\<*<8>*>/ påti.\<*<9>*>/  #<|| 8 ||>#
#<Vv_I,3[=3].3>#        Ta-y-idaü tayà Nàrada sàmaü\<*<10>*>/ diññhaü
         anukampakà ye kusalà vadeyyuü:
         mà pesuõaü mà ca musà abhàõi
         yakkho tuvaü hohisi kàmakàmã ti.  #<|| 9 ||>#
                         Påtimukhapetavatthu tatiyaü
\<&2>/

\<--------------------------------------------------------------------------
&1
     1 T sabbaso vaõõo
     2 T, (B1), (B2), (K) akarà
     3 R, T -àsiü - differences due to the non-observance of sandhi 
        in instances such as this will not be noted hereafter.
     4 R Nàradà ti
     5 (B1), (K), PvA(C, R) tàhaü
&2
     1 MSS. C1, D1 consulted by R omit these two stanzas.
     2 (S1) vehàsayaü; keci pana vihàsayaü . . ñi pàñhaü vatvà - PvA
     3 C antaëikkhe; l > ë in C and other Sinhalese sources will not 
        be  noted hereafter.
     4 R, T, PvA(R) kimiyo
     5 C, (S1) duññhavàco; R, T, PvA(R) dukkhavàco; atidukkhavàco ti 
        và pàñho - PvA
     6 C, R, (S1), PvA(R) tapassãråpo
     7 R, PvA(R) -dhàtuü
     8 R, PvA(R) pesuniyena; (P) pesukiyena. Obvious errors in the use 
        of the graphemes n / õ will not be generally noted hereafter.
     9 R, PvA påtã ti
    10 No elision of ü is attested
>/

#<Vv_I,4[=4].1>#    Yaü ki¤c' àrammaõaü katvà dajjà dànaü amaccharã
     pubbapete\<*<1>*>/ ca\<*<2>*>/ àrabbha atha và vatthudevatà;  #<|| 10 ||>#
#<Vv_I,4[=4].2>#    \<*<3>*>/Cattàro ca\<*<2>*>/ mahàràje lokapàle yasassino\<*<4>*>/
     Kuveraü Dhataraññha¤ ca Viråpakkhaü\<*<5>*>/ Viråëhakaü-
     te\<*<6>*>/ c' eva\<*<6>*>/ påjità honti dàyakà ca anipphalà.  #<|| 11 ||>#
#<Vv_I,4[=4].3>#    Na hi ruõõaü va\<*<7>*>/ soko và yà c' a¤¤à paridevanà
     na taü petassa\<*<8>*>/ atthàya evaü tiññhanti ¤àtayo.  #<|| 12 ||>#
#<Vv_I,4[=4].4>#    Aya¤ ca kho dakkhiõà dinnà saïghamhi suppatiññhità
     dãgharattaü hitày' assa ñhànaso upakappatã ti.  #<|| 13 ||>#
                      Piññhadhãtalikapetavatthu catutthaü

                            #<5 Tirokuóóapetavatthu>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].1>#    Tirokuóóesu\<*<1>*>/ tiññhanti sandhisiïghàñakesu ca
     dvàrabàhàsu tiññhanti àgantvàna sakaü gharaü.  #<|| 14 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].2>#   Pahåte annapànamhi khajjabhojje upaññhite
     na tesaü koci sarati sattànaü kammapaccayà.  #<|| 15 ||>#

\<--------------------------------------------------------------------------
&1
     1 R, T, PvA(R) pubbe pete
     2 T va
     3 C takes this line as pàdas ef of v.1. PvA(C) differs, still further.
     4 R, B, N, (B), PvA(R, B) yasassine
     5 R adds ca
     6 R tam eva
     7 R, T, (S1), PvA(B) và; PvA(R) 'va
     8 (P) petànam; cf. ver.2
>/

%<4                                   Petavatthu>%
#<Vv_I,5[=5].3>#    \<*<2>*>/Evaü dadanti ¤àtãnaü ye honti anukampakà
     suciü paõãtaü kàlena kappiyaü pànabhojanaü:
     idaü vo ¤àtãnaü\<*<3>*>/ hotu sukhità hontu ¤àtayo.  #<|| 16 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].4>#    Te ca tattha samàgantvà ¤àtipetà samàgatà
     pahåte annapànamhi sakkaccaü anumodare:  #<|| 17 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].5>#    Ciraü jãvantu no ¤àtã yesaü hetu labhàmase
     amhàka¤ ca katà påjà dàyakà ca anipphalà.  #<|| 18 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].6>#    \<*<4>*>/Na hi tattha kasã atthi gorakkh' ettha\<*<5>*>/ na vijjati
     vaõijjà tàdisã natthi hira¤¤ena\<*<6>*>/ kayakkayaü,\<*<7>*>/
     ito dinnena yàpenti petà kàlakatà\<*<8>*>/ tahiü.  #<|| 19 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].7>#    Unname udakaü\<*<9>*>/ vuññhaü\<*<10>*>/ yathà ninnaü pavattati
     evam eva ito dinnaü petànaü upakappati.  #<|| 20 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].8>#    Yathà vàrivahà pårà paripårenti sàgaraü
     evam eva ito dinnaü petànaü upakappati.  #<|| 21 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].9>#    Adàsi me akàsi me ¤àtimittà sakhà ca me
     petànaü dakkhiõaü\<*<11>*>/ dajjà pubbe katam anussaraü.  #<|| 22 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].10>#   Na hi ruõõaü va\<*<12>*>/ soko và yà c' a¤¤à paridevanà

suppatiññhità
     dãgharattaü hitày' assa ñhànaso upakappati.  #<|| 24 ||>#
#<Vv_I,5[=5].12>#       So ¤àtidhammo ca ayaü nidassito
         petànaü påjà ca katà uëàrà
         bala¤ ca bhikkhånam anuppadinnaü
         tumhehi pu¤¤aü pasutaü anappakan ti.  #<|| 25 ||>#
                         Tirokuóóapetavatthu pa¤camaü

\<--------------------------------------------------------------------------
     1 B, N, PvA(B) -kuññesu; R, PvA(R) tiro kuóóesu
     2 The arrangement of verses in R is followed here. Kh. differs: 
        (agrees with C).
     3 Kh. ¤àtinaü suits the metre.
     4 The arrangement of verses in B, N and Kh. is followed from here 
        onwards.
    5 R, (P), PvA(R, B) etta; (B2) etthe
     6 (P) hiraõyàna
     7 B, N, T, (P), PvA(B) kayàkayaü; C, (K), PvA(C) kayàkkayaü
     8 B, N, (K) kàlaïkatà; PvA(B) kàlagatà
     9 PvA(R) v' udakaü
    10 C, PvA(C) vaññhaü; Kh. vaññaü
    11 R dakkhiõà; dakkhiõà dajjà ti và pàñho - PvA
    12 As with C; R, T, B, N, PvA(B) và
    13 T petassa
    14 (P) omits
    15 (P) saïgha-
>/

#<Vv_I,6[=6].3>#    Kàlena pa¤ca puttàni sàyaü pa¤ca punàpare

#<Vv_I,6[=6].4>#    Parióayhati dhåmàyati khudàya\<*<5>*>/ hadayaü mama
     pànãyaü na labhe pàtum passa mam vyasanam gatan ti.  #<|| 29 ||>#
#<Vv_I,6[=6].5>#    Kin nu kàyena vàcàya manasà dukkañaü\<*<6>*>/ kataü\<*<7>*>/

     sàhaü paduññhamanasà akariü gabbhapàtanaü.  #<|| 31 ||>#
#<Vv_I,6[=6].7>#    Tassà dvemàsiko gabbho lohita¤ ¤eva paggharã\<*<9>*>/

     puttamaüsàni khàdàmi pubbalohitamakkhità\<*<15>*>/ ti.  #<|| 34 ||>#
                    Pa¤caputtakhàdakapetavatthu\<*<16>*>/ chattaü

\<--------------------------------------------------------------------------
     1 B, N, (P), (B1) makkhikàhi parikiõõà; (S2) -kiõõà ca, v. 35

     4 R, T na

        JPTS 1904,148 explains (P) màdayi as causative of âˆšm0rd 
        (and not as-m àdayi) but rejects the reading in his PvA(R).

     Brahmadattassa bhaddan te,\<*<6>*>/ Brahmadattassa màrisa.  #<|| 371 ||>#

     imasmiü àëàhane daóóhà tesaü kam anusocasã ti.  #<|| 373 ||>#

     taü bhante anusocàmi bhattàraü sabbakàmadaü.  #<|| 374 ||>#
